focus_tree = {
	id = STG
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = STG
		}
	}
	default = no

	continuous_focus_position = {
		x = 400
		y = 2300
	}

	initial_show_position = { ###为什么不能用了?
		#focus = STG_starting_1 
        x = 31 #30
        y = 0
        offset = {
			x = -23
			y = 5
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = STG_monarchy_abolished
                    has_country_flag = STG_monarchy_kept
                    has_country_flag = STG_army_takeover
                    has_country_flag = STG_darjeeling_route
                }
			}
		}
        offset = {
			x = -5
			y = 5
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = STG_darjeeling_route
			}
		}
	}

				NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = STG_monarchy_abolished
                    has_country_flag = STG_monarchy_kept
                    has_country_flag = STG_army_takeover
                }
			}
		}
        offset = {
            x = 14
            y = 0
            trigger = {
                has_completed_focus = STG_com_16
            }
        }
        cost = 2
        available_if_capitulated = yes
        ai_will_do = {
			#factor = 1
            factor = 100
		}
        allow_branch = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = STG_darjeeling_route
            }
        }
        completion_reward = {
			add_political_power = 50
            set_country_flag = STG_enable_parliament_events

				id = STG_centralized_vs_decentralized
				left_side = STG_centralized_vs_decentralized_left_side
				right_side = STG_centralized_vs_decentralized_right_side
				set_default = yes
			}
		}
    }
